    50	# RULES #

    52	#/
    53	# Lints files to ensure compliance with EditorConfig settings.
    54	#
    55	# @param {string} [PACKAGES_FILTER] - file path pattern (e.g., `.*/math/base/special/abs/.*`)
    56	#
    57	# @example
    58	# make lint-editorconfig
    59	#
    60	# @example
    61	# make lint-editorconfig PACKAGES_FILTER=".*/math/base/special/abs/.*"
    62	#/
    63	lint-editorconfig: $(NODE_MODULES)
    64	        $(QUIET) $(FIND_PACKAGES_CMD) | grep '^[\/]\|^[a-zA-Z]:[/\]' | while read -r pkg; do \
    65	                echo ''; \

    68	        done

    72	#/
    73	# Lints a specified list of files to ensure compliance with EditorConfig settings.
    74	#
    75	# ## Notes
    76	#
    77	# -   This rule is useful when wanting to lint a list of files generated by some other command (e.g., a list of changed files obtained via `git diff`).
    78	#
    79	# @private
    80	# @param {string} FILES - list of file paths
    81	#
    82	# @example
    83	# make lint-editorconfig-files FILES='foo/test.js bar/index.d.ts'
    84	#/
    85	lint-editorconfig-files: $(NODE_MODULES)

"""
Script to reproduce EditorConfig lint errors
"""

import subprocess
import os

def run_editorconfig_checker():
    """Run editorconfig-checker to reproduce the lint errors"""
    
    # First, let'"'"'s check if editorconfig-checker is available
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(['"'"'npx'"'"', '"'"'editorconfig-checker'"'"', '"'"'--version'"'"'], 
                              capture_output=True, text=True)
        print("editorconfig-checker version:", result.stdout.strip())
    except Exception as e:
        print("Error running editorconfig-checker:", e)
        return

    files_to_check = [
        "/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json",
        "/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json",
        "/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json"
    ]

        print(f"\nChecking file: {file_path}")
        try:
            # Check the file'"'"'s ending
            with open(file_path, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
                content = f.read()
                if not content.endswith(b'"'"'\n'"'"'):
                    print("  ❌ No final newline")
                else:
                    print("  ✓ Has final newline")
            
            # Check for tabs vs spaces
            with open(file_path, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
                lines = f.readlines()
                for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
                    if '"'"'\t'"'"' in line and not line.strip().startswith('"'"'{'"'"'):
                        print(f"  ❌ Line {i}: Contains tabs instead of spaces")
                        break
                else:
                    print("  ✓ Proper indentation")
                    
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  Error: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_editorconfig_checker()'

"""
Test script to verify the EditorConfig lint errors are fixed
"""

import subprocess
import os

def test_editorconfig_lint():
    """Test if the EditorConfig lint errors are resolved"""
    
    # Test with editorconfig-checker
    try:
        result = subprocess.run([
            '"'"'npx'"'"', '"'"'editorconfig-checker'"'"', 
            '"'"'--config'"'"', '"'"'/testbed/tools/mk/config/editorconfig-checker/.editorconfig_checker.json'"'"',
            '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"',
            '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"',
            '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"'
        ], capture_output=True, text=True)
        
        if result.returncode == 0:
            print("✅ All EditorConfig lint errors have been fixed!")
            return True
        else:
            print("❌ EditorConfig lint errors still exist:")
            print(result.stdout)
            print(result.stderr)
            return False
            
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error running editorconfig-checker: {e}")
        return False

def verify_fixes():
    """Verify the specific fixes we made"""
    
    issues_found = []
    
    # Check default.json
    with open('"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
        if '"'"'\t'"'"' in content:
            issues_found.append("defaults.json still contains tabs")
        if not content.endswith('"'"'\n'"'"'):
            issues_found.append("defaults.json missing final newline")
    
    # Check ignore_patterns.json
    with open('"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
        if '"'"'\t'"'"' in content:
            issues_found.append("ignore_patterns.json still contains tabs")
        if not content.endswith('"'"'\n'"'"'):
            issues_found.append("ignore_patterns.json missing final newline")
    
    # Check medium_positive_5.json
    with open('"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
        if not content.endswith('"'"'\n'"'"'):
            issues_found.append("medium_positive_5.json missing final newline")
    
    if issues_found:
        print("❌ Issues found:")
        for issue in issues_found:
            print(f"  - {issue}")
        return False
    else:
        print("✅ All individual checks passed!")
        return True

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("Testing EditorConfig lint fixes...")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    print("\n1. Running editorconfig-checker...")
    test1 = test_editorconfig_lint()
    
    print("\n2. Verifying individual fixes...")
    test2 = verify_fixes()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    if test1 and test2:
        print("🎉 All tests passed! The EditorConfig lint errors have been successfully fixed.")
    else:
        print("❌ Some tests failed. Please review the errors above.")'

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Script to reproduce EditorConfig lint errors
+"""
+
+import subprocess
+import os
+
+def run_editorconfig_checker():
+    """Run editorconfig-checker to reproduce the lint errors"""
+    
+    # First, let's check if editorconfig-checker is available
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run(['npx', 'editorconfig-checker', '--version'], 
+                              capture_output=True, text=True)
+        print("editorconfig-checker version:", result.stdout.strip())
+    except Exception as e:
+        print("Error running editorconfig-checker:", e)
+        return
+    
+    # Check the problematic files individually
+    files_to_check = [
+        "/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json",
+        "/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json",
+        "/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json"
+    ]
+    
+    for file_path in files_to_check:
+        print(f"\nChecking file: {file_path}")
+        try:
+            # Check the file's ending
+            with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:
+                content = f.read()
+                if not content.endswith(b'\n'):
+                    print("  ❌ No final newline")
+                else:
+                    print("  ✓ Has final newline")
+            
+            # Check for tabs vs spaces
+            with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
+                lines = f.readlines()
+                for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
+                    if '\t' in line and not line.strip().startswith('{'):
+                        print(f"  ❌ Line {i}: Contains tabs instead of spaces")
+                        break
+                else:
+                    print("  ✓ Proper indentation")
+                    
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"  Error: {e}")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    run_editorconfig_checker()
\ No newline at end of file

+# Summary of EditorConfig Lint Error Fixes
+
+## Issues Fixed
+
+1. **Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)**
+   - ✅ Fixed: `/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json`
+     - Changed tabs to 2-space indentation for JSON files as per EditorConfig rules
+   - ✅ Fixed: `/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json`
+     - Changed tabs to 2-space indentation for JSON files as per EditorConfig rules
+
+2. **Wrong line endings or no final newline**
+   - ✅ Fixed: `/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json`
+     - Added final newline at the end of the file
+
+## Changes Made
+
+### File 1: `/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json`
+- **Before**: Used tabs for indentation (violates JSON file rules)
+- **After**: Changed to 2-space indentation (compliant with EditorConfig)
+
+### File 2: `/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json`
+- **Before**: Used tabs for indentation (violates JSON file rules) 
+- **After**: Changed to 2-space indentation (compliant with EditorConfig)
+
+### File 3: `/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json`
+- **Before**: Missing final newline (violates EditorConfig rule: `insert_final_newline = true`)
+- **After**: Added final newline character
+
+## EditorConfig Rules Applied
+
+According to `/testbed/.editorconfig`:
+- **JSON files** (`*.json`):
+  - `indent_style = space`
+  - `indent_size = 2`
+  - `end_of_line = lf`
+  - `insert_final_newline = true`
+
+## Verification
+
+All fixes have been verified:
+1. ✅ EditorConfig checker passes without errors
+2. ✅ Individual file checks confirm proper indentation and line endings
+3. ✅ No tabs remain in JSON files (replaced with 2 spaces)
+4. ✅ All files end with newline characters
+
+## Impact
+
+These changes ensure compliance with the project's EditorConfig standards and will prevent similar linting failures in future CI/CD workflow runs.

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Test script to verify the EditorConfig lint errors are fixed
+"""
+
+import subprocess
+import os
+
+def test_editorconfig_lint():
+    """Test if the EditorConfig lint errors are resolved"""
+    
+    # Test with editorconfig-checker
+    try:
+        result = subprocess.run([
+            'npx', 'editorconfig-checker', 
+            '--config', '/testbed/etc/editorconfig-checker/.editorconfig_checker.json',
+            '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
+            '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json',
+            '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'
+        ], capture_output=True, text=True)
+        
+        if result.returncode == 0:
+            print("✅ All EditorConfig lint errors have been fixed!")
+            return True
+        else:
+            print("❌ EditorConfig lint errors still exist:")
+            print(result.stdout)
+            print(result.stderr)
+            return False
+            
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error running editorconfig-checker: {e}")
+        return False
+
+def verify_fixes():
+    """Verify the specific fixes we made"""
+    
+    issues_found = []
+    
+    # Check default.json
+    with open('/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json', 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+        if '\t' in content:
+            issues_found.append("defaults.json still contains tabs")
+        if not content.endswith('\n'):
+            issues_found.append("defaults.json missing final newline")
+    
+    # Check ignore_patterns.json
+    with open('/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json', 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+        if '\t' in content:
+            issues_found.append("ignore_patterns.json still contains tabs")
+        if not content.endswith('\n'):
+            issues_found.append("ignore_patterns.json missing final newline")
+    
+    # Check medium_positive_5.json
+    with open('/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json', 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+        if not content.endswith('\n'):
+            issues_found.append("medium_positive_5.json missing final newline")
+    
+    if issues_found:
+        print("❌ Issues found:")
+        for issue in issues_found:
+            print(f"  - {issue}")
+        return False
+    else:
+        print("✅ All individual checks passed!")
+        return True
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    print("Testing EditorConfig lint fixes...")
+    print("=" * 50)
+    
+    print("\n1. Running editorconfig-checker...")
+    test1 = test_editorconfig_lint()
+    
+    print("\n2. Verifying individual fixes...")
+    test2 = verify_fixes()
+    
+    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
+    if test1 and test2:
+        print("🎉 All tests passed! The EditorConfig lint errors have been successfully fixed.")
+    else:
+        print("❌ Some tests failed. Please review the errors above.")
\ No newline at end of file
